<![endif]--><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b><span style="line-height: 115%;">Spiritual (Festival) Message for the Day  Vara Lakshmi Vrata by Sri Swami Sivananda</span></b></span></p>
<p><strong><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times Digest | 8 August 2014 14.26 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><br style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;" /></span></span></strong></p>

<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
  <o:AllowPNG/>
 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
</xml><![endif]-->
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Vara Lakshmi Vrata</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Divine Life Society Publication: </b><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/hindufest.htm#_VPID_29"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Hindu Fasts and Festivals</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">LORD SHIVA describes the glory of this Vrata in the <i>Skanda Purana. </i>It is performed by a woman whose husband is still living. Maha Lakshmi is the abode of all auspiciousness and prosperity. This worship of Maha Lakshmi is done to obtain good progeny, and for the health and long life of the husband. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">The Vrata is observed on the Friday immediately preceding the full moon day of the month of Sravan (August-September). After a purificatory bath, the lady should put on a clean, fresh cloth and make a <i>mandala </i>with the drawing of a lotus upon it. A <i>kalasha </i>filled with rice and topped with fresh mango leaves, a coconut and cloth are placed on the <i>mandala </i>and Lakshmi is invoked therein. Fresh grains are used in the worship as they convey the idea of growth and prosperity. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">After the worship of the <i>kalasha, </i>follows the worship of Ganesha, then the worship of the <i>raksha </i>or the sacred thread. Now the main worship of Vara Lakshmi begins and the <i>raksha </i>is worshipped a second time. It is then tied to the right hand of the lady. After the worship various auspicious articles are given as charity to some deserving lady whose husband is alive. This lady is also fed with dainties. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Lakshmi not only bestows wealth and all sorts of material prosperity, but also imparts divine wisdom to all Her devotees. She is Vidya Shakti. She introduces Her devotees to Her Lord. She recommends them to Her Lord for their salvation. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">She is the power of Lord Narayana who is also known as Lord Vishnu or Lord Hari. Narayana is Gods aspect of preservation. He is an embodiment of Shuddha Sattwa. Lakshmi is His causal body. She is Maya, the illusory power of Nature. She deludes the whole world by Her veiling power and projects it through Her projecting power. She Herself as Vidya-Lakshmi enlightens the spiritual aspirant. Beauty, grace, a picturesque scenery or charming landscape, modesty, love, prosperity, music, the five elements and their combinations, the internal organs, mind, Prana, intellectall these are Her manifestations. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Without Lakshmi even Sannyasins cannot do propaganda or preaching work or run their institutions. They are in fact more in need of Lakshmi than the householders because they have to do great dynamic work for human weal. Sri Shankara worshipped Devi, Lakshmi and Saraswathi for success in his work. All great prophets and divine messengers who have done great spiritual work in the past were devotees of Mother Lakshmi, Devi and Saraswathi. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">May Goddess Lakshmi bless you all! Let us repeat Her Mantra: </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><i>Om mahaadevyai cha vidmahe;</i> <a name="_GoBack"></a></span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"> <i>Vishnu patnyai cha dheemahi</i> </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"> <i>Tanno lakshmi prachodayat.</i></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Excerpts from: </b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Vara Lakshmi Vrata - </b><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/hindufest.htm#_VPID_29"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Hindu Fasts and Festivals</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Additional Reading<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">: Daily Invocations - </b><a href="http://www.swami-krishnananda.org/invoc/in_sria.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Sri Sukta</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Swami Krishnananda</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
